<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:анатомический.html>анатоми́ческий</a> (16499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анатомия.html>анато́мия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anatómija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анатомический.html>анатоми́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">anatomíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>anatomical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анатомический.html>анатоми́ческий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">anatomíčeskij teátr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dissecting room</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ана́том</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">anátom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***анафема.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a> (27756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνάθεμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anáthema</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">anáfema</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фемы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фемы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фем</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>anathema, excommunication</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scolding word
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">макси́м <a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рький</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Maksím Górʹkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,  <cite><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Tróje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></cite>  | <cite>The Three</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Лунёв <a href = vnd.unilang:молчать.html>молча́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ненавидеть.html>ненави́дя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душо́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мал</a>: «<a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>Хоть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:анафема.html>ана́фема</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вывихнуть.html>вы́вихнула</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прыгать.html>пры́гая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a>...»</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lunjóv molčál i, nenavídja jejó vsej dušój, dúmal: “Xotʹ by ty, <b>anáfema</b>, nógu sebé vývixnula, prýgaja tut...”</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Lunyov was silent and, hating her with his whole heart, thought: "<b>Anathema</b>, I wish you you dislocated your leg, jumping here ...”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ангина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ангина.html>анги́на</a> (16354)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангина.html>анги́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">angína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангина.html>анги́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангина.html>анги́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ангина.html>анги́н</a></b>)
</p>

***английский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>английский</a> (1214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">а́нглия</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ánglija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́йский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">anglíjskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>English
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>anglíjskij</b> jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the English language</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йские</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:белила.html>бели́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>anglíjskije</b> belíla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">white lead</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>anglíjskaja</b> boléznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rickets</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:булавка.html>була́вка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>anglíjskaja</b> bulávka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">safety pin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>anglíjskij</b> zamók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">patent lock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соль.html>соль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>anglíjskaja</b> solʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Epsom salts</span></div></dd>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">anecdote</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анемия.html>анеми́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">anemíja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анемия.html>анеми́и</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аннулировать.html>аннули́ровать</a> (26390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аннулировать.html>аннули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">annulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:анонимка.html>анони́мка</a> (25849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">анони́м(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anoním(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from an ellipsis of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анонимный.html>анони́мное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письмо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anonímnoje pisʹmó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anonymous letter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анонимка.html>анони́мка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">anonímka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анонимка.html>анони́мки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анонимка.html>анони́мки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анонимка.html>анони́мок</a></b>)
</p>
